/*
1. Use a consistent sensible line-height in all browsers.
2. Prevent adjustments of font size after orientation changes in iOS.
3. Use a more readable tab size.
4. Use the user's configured `sans` font-family by default.
5. Use the user's configured `sans` font-feature-settings by default.
6. Use the user's configured `sans` font-variation-settings by default.
7. Disable tap highlights on iOS
*/

html,
:host {
  line-height: 1.5; /* 1 */
  -webkit-text-size-adjust: 100%; /* 2 */
  -moz-tab-size: 4; /* 3 */
  tab-size: 4; /* 3 */
  font-family: ui-sans-serif, system-ui, sans-serif, "Apple Color Emoji", "Segoe UI Emoji", "Segoe UI Symbol", "Noto Color Emoji"; /* 4 */
  font-feature-settings: normal; /* 5 */
  font-variation-settings: normal; /* 6 */
  -webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; /* 7 */
}

/*
1. Remove the margin in all browsers.
2. Inherit line-height from `html` so users can set them as a class directly on the `html` element.
*/

  margin: 0; /* 1 */
  line-height: inherit; /* 2 */
}

1. Add the correct height in Firefox.

}

  // virtual:/components/commom/category/category-products-section.tsx
  var cssReady = false;
  function ensureCSS() {
    if (cssReady) return;
    cssReady = true;
    const s = document.createElement("style");
    s.textContent = "[data-rv]{opacity:0;transform:translateY(20px)}[data-rv].rv{animation:rvUp .3s ease-out forwards;animation-delay:calc(var(--d)*1s)}@keyframes rvUp{to{opacity:1;transform:translateY(0)}}";
    document.head.appendChild(s);
  }
  var cachedCols = 0;
  var cachedWidth = 0;
  function getCols() {
    const w = window.innerWidth;
    if (w === cachedWidth) return cachedCols;
    cachedWidth = w;
    cachedCols = w >= 1024 ? 5 : w >= 768 ? 4 : w >= 640 ? 3 : 2;
    return cachedCols;
  }
  var obs = null;
  var cbs = /* @__PURE__ */ new Map();
  function getObs() {
    if (obs) return obs;
    obs = new IntersectionObserver(
      (entries) => {
        for (let i = 0; i < entries.length; i++) {
          if (!entries[i].isIntersecting) continue;
          const t = entries[i].target;
          const cb = cbs.get(t);
          if (cb) {
            cb();
            cbs.delete(t);
            obs.unobserve(t);
          } else if (t.dataset.rv != null) {
            t.classList.add("rv");
            cbs.delete(t);
            obs.unobserve(t);
          }
        }
        if (cbs.size === 0 && obs) {
          obs.disconnect();
          obs = null;
        }
      },
      { threshold: 0.05, rootMargin: "60px 0px" }
    );
    return obs;
  }
  function startObserve(el, cb) {
    cbs.set(el, cb);
    getObs().observe(el);
  }
  function stopObserve(el) {
    cbs.delete(el);
    if (obs) {
      obs.unobserve(el);
      if (cbs.size === 0) {
        obs.disconnect();
        obs = null;
      }
    }
  }
  function RevealCard({ children, index }) {
    const ref = React.useRef(null);
    React.useEffect(() => {
      ensureCSS();
      const el = ref.current;
      if (!el) return;
      const col = index % getCols();
      el.style.setProperty("--d", String(col * 0.18));
      startObserve(el, null);
      return () => stopObserve(el);
    }, [index]);
    return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { ref, "data-rv": true }, children);
  }
  function sortProducts(products = []) {
    return [...products].sort((a, b) => {
      const catA = Number(a?.category?.position);
      const catB = Number(b?.category?.position);
      const prodA = Number(a?.settings?.position);
      const prodB = Number(b?.settings?.position);
      const hCatA = Number.isFinite(catA);
      const hCatB = Number.isFinite(catB);
      const hProdA = Number.isFinite(prodA);
      const hProdB = Number.isFinite(prodB);
      if (hCatA && hCatB && catA !== catB) return catA - catB;
      if (hCatA && !hCatB) return -1;
      if (!hCatA && hCatB) return 1;
      if (hProdA && hProdB && prodA !== prodB) return prodA - prodB;
      if (hProdA && !hProdB) return -1;
      if (!hProdA && hProdB) return 1;
      return 0;
    });
  }

  // virtual:/hooks/use-floating.tsx
  function parsePlacement(placement) {
    const [base, align] = placement.split("-");
    return { base, align: align || "start" };
  }
  function getRect(el) {
    return el ? el.getBoundingClientRect() : null;
  }
  function clamp(val, min, max) {
    return Math.max(min, Math.min(max, val));
  }
  function opp(base) {
    switch (base) {
      case "top":
        return "bottom";
      case "bottom":
        return "top";
      case "left":
        return "right";
      case "right":
        return "left";
    }
  }
  function computeCoords({
    referenceRect,
    floatingRect,
    base,
    align,
    offset
  }) {
    let x = 0;
    let y = 0;
    if (base === "top") {
      y = referenceRect.top - floatingRect.height - offset;
    } else if (base === "bottom") {
      y = referenceRect.bottom + offset;
    } else if (base === "left") {
      x = referenceRect.left - floatingRect.width - offset;
    } else if (base === "right") {
      x = referenceRect.right + offset;
    }
    if (base === "top" || base === "bottom") {
      if (align === "start") {
        x = referenceRect.left;
      } else if (align === "center") {
        x = referenceRect.left + (referenceRect.width - floatingRect.width) / 2;
      } else {
        x = referenceRect.right - floatingRect.width;
      }
    } else {
      if (align === "start") {
        y = referenceRect.top;
      } else if (align === "center") {
        y = referenceRect.top + (referenceRect.height - floatingRect.height) / 2;
      } else {
        y = referenceRect.bottom - floatingRect.height;
      }
    }
    return { x, y };
  }
  function getOverflow({
    x,
    y,
    floatingRect,
    padding = 0
  }) {
    const leftOverflow = x - padding;
    const topOverflow = y - padding;
    const rightOverflow = x + floatingRect.width + padding - window.innerWidth;
    const bottomOverflow = y + floatingRect.height + padding - window.innerHeight;
    return {
      left: leftOverflow < 0 ? -leftOverflow : 0,
      top: topOverflow < 0 ? -topOverflow : 0,
      right: rightOverflow > 0 ? rightOverflow : 0,
      bottom: bottomOverflow > 0 ? bottomOverflow : 0,
      any: leftOverflow < 0 || topOverflow < 0 || rightOverflow > 0 || bottomOverflow > 0
    };
  }
  function useFloating(options = {}) {
    const {
      placement = "bottom-start",
      offset = 8,
      flip = true,
      shiftPadding = 8,
      whileElementsMounted = true
    } = options;
    const referenceRef = React.useRef(null);
    const floatingRef = React.useRef(null);
    const placementRef = React.useRef(placement);
    placementRef.current = placement;
    const updateRef = React.useRef(() => {
    });
    const [floatingStyles, setFloatingStyles] = React.useState({
      position: "fixed",
      left: -9999,
      top: -9999,
      visibility: "hidden"
      // <-- importante
    });
    const compute = React.useCallback(() => {
      const refEl = referenceRef.current;
      const floatEl = floatingRef.current;
      if (!refEl || !floatEl) return;
      const referenceRect = getRect(refEl);
      const floatingRect = getRect(floatEl);
      const { base, align } = parsePlacement(placementRef.current);
      let { x, y } = computeCoords({ referenceRect, floatingRect, base, align, offset });
      let overflow = getOverflow({ x, y, floatingRect, padding: shiftPadding });
      if (flip && overflow.any) {
        const oppositeBase = opp(base);
        const { x: x2, y: y2 } = computeCoords({
          referenceRect,
          floatingRect,
          base: oppositeBase,
          align,
          offset
        });
        const overflowOpp = getOverflow({ x: x2, y: y2, floatingRect, padding: shiftPadding });
        const sumOverflow = overflow.left + overflow.top + overflow.right + overflow.bottom;
        const sumOpp = overflowOpp.left + overflowOpp.top + overflowOpp.right + overflowOpp.bottom;
        if (sumOpp < sumOverflow) {
          ({ x, y } = { x: x2, y: y2 });
          overflow = overflowOpp;
        }
      }
      const minX = shiftPadding;
      const maxX = window.innerWidth - floatingRect.width - shiftPadding;
      const minY = shiftPadding;
      const maxY = window.innerHeight - floatingRect.height - shiftPadding;
      x = clamp(x, minX, Math.max(minX, maxX));
      y = clamp(y, minY, Math.max(minY, maxY));
      setFloatingStyles({
        position: "fixed",
        left: Math.round(x),
        top: Math.round(y),
        visibility: "visible"
      });
    }, [offset, flip, shiftPadding]);
    React.useEffect(() => {
      updateRef.current = compute;
    }, [compute]);
    React.useEffect(() => {
      if (!whileElementsMounted) return;
      let roRef = null;
      const handle = () => updateRef.current();
      if (referenceRef.current && floatingRef.current) {
        roRef = new ResizeObserver(handle);
        roRef.observe(referenceRef.current);
        roRef.observe(floatingRef.current);
      }
      window.addEventListener("resize", handle);
      window.addEventListener("scroll", handle, true);
      const interval = setInterval(handle, 200);
      return () => {
        if (roRef) {
          try {
            roRef.disconnect();
          } catch {
          }
          roRef = null;
        }
        window.removeEventListener("resize", handle);
        window.removeEventListener("scroll", handle, true);
        clearInterval(interval);
      };
    }, [whileElementsMounted]);
    const setReference = React.useCallback((node) => {
      referenceRef.current = node;
      requestAnimationFrame(() => updateRef.current());
    }, []);
    const setFloating = React.useCallback((node) => {
      floatingRef.current = node;
      requestAnimationFrame(() => updateRef.current());
    }, []);
    const update = React.useCallback(() => updateRef.current(), []);
    return {
      refs: {
        setReference,
        setFloating,
        reference: referenceRef,
        floating: floatingRef
      },
      floatingStyles,
      update
    };
  }

  function SocialMediaPopoverButton({
    socialMedias,
    className
  }) {
    const [open, setOpen] = React.useState(false);
    const { refs, floatingStyles } = useFloating({
      placement: "bottom-end",
      offset: 8,
      flip: true,
      shiftPadding: 8
    });
    React.useEffect(() => {
      if (!open) return;
      function handleClick(e) {
        if (refs.reference.current?.contains(e.target) || refs.floating.current?.contains(e.target))
          return;
        setOpen(false);
      }
      function handleEsc(e) {
        if (e.key === "Escape") setOpen(false);
      }
      document.addEventListener("mousedown", handleClick);
      document.addEventListener("keydown", handleEsc);
      return () => {
        document.removeEventListener("mousedown", handleClick);
        document.removeEventListener("keydown", handleEsc);
      };
    }, [open]);
    return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(React.Fragment, null, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(

  var { useRef, useState, useEffect, useCallback } = React;
  function CategoryCarousel({
    categories,
    scrollToRef,
    onOverflowChange
  }) {
    const scrollContainerRef = useRef(null);
    const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);
    const [startX, setStartX] = useState(0);
    const [scrollLeft, setScrollLeft] = useState(0);
    const handleMouseDown = (e) => {
      setIsDragging(true);
      setStartX(e.pageX - (scrollContainerRef.current?.offsetLeft || 0));
      setScrollLeft(scrollContainerRef.current?.scrollLeft || 0);
      e.preventDefault();
    };
    const handleMouseMove = (e) => {
      if (!isDragging || !scrollContainerRef.current) return;
      const x = e.pageX - (scrollContainerRef.current?.offsetLeft || 0);
      const walk = (x - startX) * 1.5;
      scrollContainerRef.current.scrollLeft = scrollLeft - walk;
    };
    const handleMouseUp = () => {
      setIsDragging(false);
    };
    const checkOverflow = useCallback(() => {
      const container = scrollContainerRef.current;
      if (!container || !onOverflowChange) return;
      onOverflowChange(container.scrollWidth > container.clientWidth + 10);
    }, [onOverflowChange]);
    const scroll = (direction) => {
      const container = scrollContainerRef.current;
      if (!container) return;
      const scrollAmount = 300;
      container.scrollBy({
        left: direction === "left" ? -scrollAmount : scrollAmount,
        behavior: "smooth"
      });
    };
    useEffect(() => {
      scrollToRef.current = scroll;
    }, []);
    useEffect(() => {
      checkOverflow();
      window.addEventListener("resize", checkOverflow);
      return () => window.removeEventListener("resize", checkOverflow);
    }, [checkOverflow, categories]);
    useEffect(() => {
      const container = scrollContainerRef.current;
      if (!container) return;
      document.addEventListener("mousemove", handleMouseMove);
      document.addEventListener("mouseup", handleMouseUp);
      container.addEventListener("mouseleave", handleMouseUp);
      return () => {
        document.removeEventListener("mousemove", handleMouseMove);
        document.removeEventListener("mouseup", handleMouseUp);
        container.removeEventListener("mouseleave", handleMouseUp);
      };
    }, [isDragging, startX, scrollLeft]);
    return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { className: "relative w-full " }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(
      "div",
      {
        ref: scrollContainerRef,
        onMouseDown: handleMouseDown,
        className: `flex gap-4 overflow-x-auto scroll-smooth scrollbar-hide w-full user-select-none ${isDragging ? "cursor-grabbing" : "cursor-grab"}`,
        style: {
          msOverflowStyle: "none",
          scrollbarWidth: "none",
          scrollSnapType: "x mandatory"
        }
      },
      categories.map((category, index) => /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(
        "div",
        {
          key: index,
          className: "flex-shrink-0 scroll-snap-align-start w-36",
          style: { scrollSnapAlign: "start" }
        },
        /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(CategoryCard, { category })
      )),
      /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("style", null, `
          .scrollbar-hide::-webkit-scrollbar {
            display: none;
          }
        `)
    ));
  }

  function FeedbacksCarousel() {
    const { sharpifyApi, isSsr } = useContext(SharpifyApi.SharpifyReact.TemplateContext);
    const [feedbacks, setFeedbacks] = useState2([]);
    const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState2(true);
    const containerRef = useRef2(null);
    const intervalRef = useRef2(null);
    const isDragging = useRef2(false);
    const wasDragging = useRef2(false);
    const startX = useRef2(0);
    const scrollStart = useRef2(0);
    if (isSsr) return null;
    useEffect2(() => {
      async function fetchFeedbacks() {
        try {
          const result = await SharpifyApi.SharpifyReact.ReactQueryAdapter(
            sharpifyApi.api.v1.checkout.feedback.listStoreFeedbacks({
              limit: 20,
              page: 1
            })
          );
          if (result?.feedbacks) {
            const filtered = result.feedbacks.filter(
              (f) => f.rating >= 4 && f.content
            );
            setFeedbacks(filtered);
          }
        } catch (e) {
          console.error("Failed to fetch feedbacks:", e);
        } finally {
          setIsLoading(false);
        }
      }
      fetchFeedbacks();
    }, []);
    function startAutoScroll() {
      if (intervalRef.current) return;
      intervalRef.current = setInterval(() => {
        const el = containerRef.current;
        if (!el || isDragging.current) return;
        el.scrollLeft += 1;
        const half = el.scrollWidth / 2;
        if (el.scrollLeft >= half) {
          el.scrollLeft -= half;
        }
      }, 20);
    }
    function stopAutoScroll() {
      if (intervalRef.current) {
        clearInterval(intervalRef.current);
        intervalRef.current = null;
      }
    }
    useEffect2(() => {
      if (feedbacks.length === 0) return;
      startAutoScroll();
      return () => stopAutoScroll();
    }, [feedbacks]);
    function onMouseDown(e) {
      isDragging.current = true;
      wasDragging.current = false;
      startX.current = e.clientX;
      scrollStart.current = containerRef.current?.scrollLeft || 0;
      stopAutoScroll();
    }
    function onMouseMove(e) {
      if (!isDragging.current || !containerRef.current) return;
      e.preventDefault();
      const dx = e.clientX - startX.current;
      if (Math.abs(dx) > 3) wasDragging.current = true;
      containerRef.current.scrollLeft = scrollStart.current - dx;
    }
    function onMouseUp() {
      if (!isDragging.current) return;
      isDragging.current = false;
      startAutoScroll();
    }
    function onTouchStart(e) {
      isDragging.current = true;
      startX.current = e.touches[0].clientX;
      scrollStart.current = containerRef.current?.scrollLeft || 0;
      stopAutoScroll();
    }
    function onTouchMove(e) {
      if (!isDragging.current || !containerRef.current) return;
      const dx = e.touches[0].clientX - startX.current;
      containerRef.current.scrollLeft = scrollStart.current - dx;
    }
    function onTouchEnd() {
      isDragging.current = false;
      setTimeout(() => startAutoScroll(), 2e3);
    }
    if (isLoading) return null;
    if (feedbacks.length === 0) return null;
    const duplicated = [...feedbacks, ...feedbacks];
    const hideScrollbarCSS = `
        .feedbacks-scroll::-webkit-scrollbar { display: none; }
    `;
    return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("section", { className: "py-8" }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("style", { dangerouslySetInnerHTML: { __html: hideScrollbarCSS } }), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { className: "border-t border-border pt-8" }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { className: "flex items-center justify-center gap-3 mb-6" }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { className: "w-10 h-10 rounded-xl bg-yellow-500/10 border border-yellow-500/20 flex items-center justify-center" }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("svg", { xmlns: "http://www.w3.org/2000/svg", width: "20", height: "20", viewBox: "0 0 24 24", fill: "currentColor", stroke: "currentColor", strokeWidth: "0", className: "text-yellow-400" }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("polygon", { points: "12 2 15.09 8.26 22 9.27 17 14.14 18.18 21.02 12 17.77 5.82 21.02 7 14.14 2 9.27 8.91 8.26 12 2" }))), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { className: "text-center" }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("h2", { className: "text-xl font-bold" }, "Avalia\xE7\xF5es dos clientes"), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("p", { className: "text-sm text-muted-foreground" }, "Veja o que nossos clientes est\xE3o dizendo")))), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(
      "div",
      {
        ref: containerRef,
        className: "feedbacks-scroll flex gap-4 overflow-x-scroll cursor-grab active:cursor-grabbing",
        style: { scrollbarWidth: "none" },
        onMouseDown,
        onMouseMove,
        onMouseUp,
        onMouseLeave: onMouseUp,
        onTouchStart,
        onTouchMove,
        onTouchEnd
      },
      duplicated.map((feedback, index) => /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(FeedbackCard, { feedback, key: `${feedback.id}-${index}` }))
    ));
  }

  function formatPrice(amount, currency = "BRL") {
    const isSsr = window.isSsr;
    if (isSsr) return `R$ ${amount}`;
    return amount.toLocaleString(void 0, {
      style: "currency",

    });

  function setCookie({ days, name, value }) {
    const date = /* @__PURE__ */ new Date();
    date.setTime(date.getTime() + days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1e3);
    const expires = "expires=" + date.toUTCString();
    window.document.cookie = `${name}=${encodeURIComponent(value)}; ${expires}; path=/`;
  }
  function deleteCookie({ name }) {
    window.document.cookie = `${name}=; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:00 UTC; path=/;`;
  }

  function Dialog({ open, onOpenChange, children }) {
    if (!open) return null;
    return ReactDOM.createPortal(
      /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(React.Fragment, null, React.Children.map(children, (child) => {
        if (React.isValidElement(child)) {
          return React.cloneElement(child, {
            onClose: () => onOpenChange(false)
          });
        }
        return child;
      })),
      document.body
    );
  }

    }, [onClose]);

        "div",

  // virtual:/components/commom/product/cart/index.tsx
  function ProductCartList({ className, productCardClassName }) {
    const { productCartItems, isProductCartItemsLoading } = React.useContext(getCartContext());
    const mappedProductCartItems = React.useMemo(() => {
      return productCartItems.reduce((acc, item) => {
        if (item.product.settings.viewType === "NORMAL") {
          acc.push({ ...item, dynamicItems: [] });
          return acc;
        }
        const existing = acc.find((i) => i.product.id === item.product.id);
        if (existing) existing.dynamicItems = [...existing.dynamicItems, item];
        else {
          acc.push({
            ...item,
            dynamicItems: [item]
          });
        }
        return acc;
      }, []);
    }, [productCartItems]);
    return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { className: cn(className) }, isProductCartItemsLoading && /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(LoadingContent, null), !isProductCartItemsLoading && /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { className: "flex flex-col gap-2 overflow-x-auto sm:overflow-x-hidden" }, mappedProductCartItems.map(({ dynamicItems, ...props }, index) => /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(
      ProductCard,
      {
        className: productCardClassName,
        productCartItem: props,
        dynamicItems,
        key: index
      }
    ))));
  }

  // virtual:/hooks/use-local-storage.tsx
  function useLocalStorage(key, initialValue) {
    const [value, setValue] = React.useState(() => {
      if (typeof window === "undefined") return initialValue;
      try {
        const item = window.localStorage.getItem(key);
        return item ? JSON.parse(item) : initialValue;
      } catch {
        return initialValue;
      }
    });
    React.useEffect(() => {
      try {
        window.localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(value));
      } catch {
      }
    }, [key, value]);
    React.useEffect(() => {
      function handleStorage(event) {
        if (event.key === key && event.newValue !== null) {
          try {
            setValue(JSON.parse(event.newValue));
          } catch {
          }
        }
      }
      window.addEventListener("storage", handleStorage);
      return () => window.removeEventListener("storage", handleStorage);
    }, [key]);
    return [value, setValue];
  }

  // virtual:/contexts/cart/helpers/find-product-item-by-id.helper.ts
  function findProductItemById({
    product,
    productItemId,
    onlyDynamic = false
  }) {
    if (product.settings.viewType === "DYNAMIC") {
      return product.dynamicItems.find((dynamicItem) => dynamicItem.id === productItemId) || null;
    }
    if (onlyDynamic) return null;
    return product.normalItem.id === productItemId ? product.normalItem : null;
  }

  // virtual:/contexts/cart/functions/add-cart-item.ts
  var makeAddCartItemFunction = ({
    cartItems,
    setCartItems
  }) => {
    const addCartItem = ({
      product,
      ...item
    }) => {
      const hasItem = (cartItems || []).find(
        (cartItem) => cartItem.productId === cartItem.productId && cartItem.productItemId === item.productItemId
      );
      if (hasItem) return;
      setCartItems((value) => {
        return [...value, item].filter(Boolean);
      });
      const productItem = findProductItemById({
        product,
        productItemId: item.productItemId
      });
      const isDynamic = product.settings.viewType === "DYNAMIC";
      const productName = isDynamic ? `${product.info.title} > ${productItem?.info?.title}` : product.info.title;
      window.dispatchEvent(
        new CustomEvent("sharpify:add-to-cart", {
          detail: {
            product: {
              id: `${item.productId}:${item.productItemId}`,
              name: productName,
              value: productItem?.pricing?.price ?? 0
            },
            currency: "BRL"
          }
        })
      );
    };
    return { addCartItem };
  };

  // virtual:/contexts/cart/functions/update-quantity.ts
  var makeUpdateQuantityFunction = ({
    setCartItems,
    productCartItems
  }) => {
    const updateQuantity = (item) => {
      const productCartItem = productCartItems.find(
        (pcItem) => pcItem.product.id === item.productId
      );
      if (!productCartItem) return;
      const productIitem = findProductItemById({
        product: productCartItem.product,
        productItemId: item.productItemId
      });
      if (!productIitem) return;
      const stockAvailable = productIitem.inventory.stockQuantity;
      const quantity = stockAvailable === null ? item.quantity > 999 ? 999 : item.quantity : stockAvailable < item.quantity ? stockAvailable : item.quantity;
      setCartItems((value) => {
        value = value.filter(Boolean);
        const stateItemIndex = value.findIndex(
          (cartItem) => cartItem.productId === item.productId && cartItem.productItemId === item.productItemId
        );
        if (stateItemIndex < 0) return value;
        if (quantity < 1) delete value[stateItemIndex];
        else value[stateItemIndex] = { ...item, quantity };
        return [...value].filter(Boolean);
      });
    };
    return { updateQuantity };
  };

  // virtual:/contexts/cart/helpers/remove-cart-item.helper.ts
  function RemoveCartItemHelper({
    setCartItems,
    productId,
    productItemId
  }) {
    setCartItems((value) => {
      value = value.filter(Boolean);
      const stateItemIndex = value.findIndex(
        (cartItem) => cartItem.productId === productId && cartItem.productItemId === productItemId
      );
      if (stateItemIndex < 0) return value;
      delete value[stateItemIndex];
      return [...value].filter(Boolean);
    });
  }

        setDragX(0);
      }

  var ToastProvider = ({
    children,
    isSsr
  }) => {
    if (isSsr) return children;
    const [toasts, setToasts] = useState2([]);
    const removeToast = (id) => {
      setToasts((prev) => prev.filter((t) => t.id !== id));
    };
    const triggerToast = (toast) => {
      const id = ++toastCounter;
      const duration = toast.duration ?? 5e3;
      setToasts((prev) => [...prev, { id, ...toast, duration }]);
      setTimeout(() => removeToast(id), duration + 300);
    };
    const toastsByPosition = toasts.reduce(
      (acc, toast) => {
        const pos = toast.position || "bottom-right";
        acc[pos].push(toast);
        return acc;
      },
      { "bottom-right": [], "top-right": [], "top-left": [], "bottom-left": [] }
    );
    return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(ToastContext.Provider, { value: { triggerToast } }, children, Object.entries(toastsByPosition).map(

    ));
  };
  var getToastContext = () => {

  // virtual:/contexts/cart/hooks/use-product-items.ts
  function UseProductItems({
    cartItems,
    setCartItems,
    coupon,
    setCoupon
  }) {
    const { store, sharpifyApi } = React.useContext(SharpifyApi.SharpifyReact.TemplateContext);
    const { triggerToast } = React.useContext(getToastContext());
    const [cachedProducts, setCachedProducts] = React.useState([]);
    const [isFetched, setIsFetched] = React.useState(false);
    const fetchedProductIdsRef = React.useRef(/* @__PURE__ */ new Set());
    const refetch = React.useCallback(async () => {
      const currentProductIds = [...new Set(cartItems.map((item) => item.productId))];
      const newProductIds = currentProductIds.filter((id) => !fetchedProductIdsRef.current.has(id));
      if (newProductIds.length === 0 && isFetched) {
        return;
      }
      const idsToFetch = newProductIds.length > 0 ? newProductIds : currentProductIds;
      if (idsToFetch.length === 0) {
        setIsFetched(true);
        return;
      }
      const result = await SharpifyApi.SharpifyReact.ReactQueryAdapter(
        sharpifyApi.api.v1.catalog.product.list({
          limit: 999,
          page: 1,
          ids: idsToFetch
        })
      );
      if (result?.products) {
        idsToFetch.forEach((id) => fetchedProductIdsRef.current.add(id));
        const returnedIds = new Set(result.products.map((p) => p.id));
        const missingIds = idsToFetch.filter((id) => !returnedIds.has(id));
        if (missingIds.length > 0) {
          setCartItems(
            (current) => current.filter((item) => !missingIds.includes(item.productId))
          );
        }
        setCachedProducts((prev) => {
          const updated = prev.filter((p) => !idsToFetch.includes(p.id) || returnedIds.has(p.id));
          const existingIds = new Set(updated.map((p) => p.id));
          const newProducts = result.products.filter((p) => !existingIds.has(p.id));
          return [...updated, ...newProducts];
        });
      }
      setIsFetched(true);
    }, [cartItems, sharpifyApi, isFetched]);
    const productCartItems = React.useMemo(() => {
      if (cachedProducts.length === 0) return [];
      let productCartItems2 = [];
      const products = cachedProducts;
      const allProductsWithCouponApplied = products.filter(
        (product) => coupon?.useCondition?.productIds?.includes(product.id)
      );
      if (coupon && !allProductsWithCouponApplied.length) {
        setCoupon(null);
        triggerToast({ message: "Nenhum produto para aplicar cupom", type: "error" });
      }
      let fixedDiscountPerProduct = 0;
      let fixedDiscountRemainder = 0;
      if (coupon?.type === "FIXED" && allProductsWithCouponApplied.length > 0) {
        fixedDiscountPerProduct = coupon?.amout / allProductsWithCouponApplied.length;
        if (fixedDiscountPerProduct < 0.01) fixedDiscountPerProduct = 0;
      }
      for (const cartItem of cartItems) {
        const isCouponApplied = !!allProductsWithCouponApplied.find(
          (p) => p.id === cartItem.productId
        );
        const product = products.find((product2) => {
          return product2.id === cartItem.productId;
        });
        if (!product) {
          if (isFetched && fetchedProductIdsRef.current.has(cartItem.productId)) {
            RemoveCartItemHelper({
              setCartItems,
              productId: cartItem.productId,
              productItemId: cartItem.productItemId
            });
          }
          continue;
        }
        const item = findProductItemById({
          product,
          productItemId: cartItem.productItemId
        });
        if (!item) {
          setCartItems((current) => {
            return current.filter(
              (i) => !(i.productId === cartItem.productId && i.productItemId === cartItem.productItemId)
            );
          });
          continue;
        }
        const subTotal = item.pricing.price * cartItem.quantity;
        let total = subTotal;
        let discountAmount = 0;
        if (coupon && isCouponApplied) {
          if (coupon.type === "PERCENTAGE") {
            discountAmount = total * coupon.amout / 100;
            total = total - discountAmount;
          } else if (coupon.type === "FIXED") {
            discountAmount = fixedDiscountPerProduct;
            total = total - discountAmount - fixedDiscountRemainder;
            fixedDiscountRemainder = 0;
            if (total < 0) {
              fixedDiscountRemainder += Math.abs(total);
              total = 0;
            }
          }
        }
        const productCartItemProps = {
          product,
          productItem: {
            props: item,
            cartItem,
            pricing: {
              total,
              subTotal,
              discountAmount,
              isCouponApplied
            }
          }
        };
        productCartItems2.push(productCartItemProps);
        if (item.inventory.stockQuantity !== null && item.inventory.stockQuantity <= 0) {
          RemoveCartItemHelper({
            setCartItems,
            productId: cartItem.productId,
            productItemId: cartItem.productItemId
          });
        }
      }
      return productCartItems2;
    }, [cachedProducts, cartItems, coupon]);
    return { productCartItems, data: { products: cachedProducts }, refetch, isLoading: !isFetched, isFetched };
  }

  // virtual:/contexts/cart/hooks/use-total-price.ts
  function useTotalPrice({
    productCartItems
  }) {
    const subTotalPrice = React.useMemo(() => {
      return productCartItems.reduce((acc, currentValue) => {
        return acc += currentValue.productItem.pricing.subTotal;
      }, 0);
    }, [productCartItems]);
    const totalPrice = React.useMemo(() => {
      return productCartItems.reduce((acc, currentValue) => {
        return acc += currentValue.productItem.pricing.total;
      }, 0);
    }, [productCartItems]);
    return { totalPrice, subTotalPrice };
  }

  // virtual:/contexts/cart/provider.tsx
  function CartProvider({ children }) {
    const { createContext: createContext2, useContext: useContext3, useEffect: useEffect6, useMemo, useState: useState5, useRef: useRef5 } = React;
    const { isSsr } = useContext3(SharpifyApi.SharpifyReact.TemplateContext);
    if (isSsr) return children;
    const pathname = window.location.pathname;
    const [open, setOpen] = useState5(false);
    const [coupon, setCoupon] = useState5(null);
    const [state, setState] = useLocalStorage("cartItems", []);
    const prevProductIdsRef = useRef5(new Set((state || []).map((item) => item.productId)));
    const { productCartItems, isLoading, isFetched, refetch, data } = UseProductItems({
      cartItems: state,
      setCartItems: setState,
      coupon,
      setCoupon
    });
    useEffect6(() => {
      const currentProductIds = new Set((state || []).map((item) => item.productId));
      const prevProductIds = prevProductIdsRef.current;
      const hasNewProduct = [...currentProductIds].some((id) => !prevProductIds.has(id));
      prevProductIdsRef.current = currentProductIds;
      if (!isFetched || open || hasNewProduct) refetch();
    }, [open, isFetched, state, pathname]);
    const { totalPrice, subTotalPrice } = useTotalPrice({
      productCartItems,
      coupon,
      cartItems: state,
      data
    });
    const { addCartItem } = makeAddCartItemFunction({ cartItems: state, setCartItems: setState });
    const { updateQuantity } = makeUpdateQuantityFunction({
      setCartItems: setState,
      productCartItems
    });
    const clearCart = () => {
      try {
        setState([]);
        setCoupon(null);
      } catch {
      }
    };
    return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(
      CartContext.Provider,
      {
        value: {
          open,
          setOpen,
          isProductCartItemsLoading: isLoading,
          cartItems: state || [],
          addCartItem,
          updateQuantity,
          productCartItems,
          totalPrice,
          subTotalPrice,
          coupon,
          setCoupon,
          clearCart
        }
      },
      /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(CartDialog, null),
      children
    );
  }

  // virtual:/hooks/use-debounce.tsx
  function useDebounce({ onComplete, time = 300, value }) {
    React.useEffect(() => {
      const timeout = setTimeout(() => onComplete(value), time);
      return () => clearTimeout(timeout);
    }, [value]);
  }

  // virtual:/hooks/use-floating.tsx
  function parsePlacement(placement) {
    const [base, align] = placement.split("-");
    return { base, align: align || "start" };
  }
  function getRect(el) {
    return el ? el.getBoundingClientRect() : null;
  }
  function clamp(val, min, max) {
    return Math.max(min, Math.min(max, val));
  }
  function opp(base) {
    switch (base) {
      case "top":
        return "bottom";
      case "bottom":
        return "top";
      case "left":
        return "right";
      case "right":
        return "left";
    }
  }
  function computeCoords({
    referenceRect,
    floatingRect,
    base,
    align,
    offset
  }) {
    let x = 0;
    let y = 0;
    if (base === "top") {
      y = referenceRect.top - floatingRect.height - offset;
    } else if (base === "bottom") {
      y = referenceRect.bottom + offset;
    } else if (base === "left") {
      x = referenceRect.left - floatingRect.width - offset;
    } else if (base === "right") {
      x = referenceRect.right + offset;
    }
    if (base === "top" || base === "bottom") {
      if (align === "start") {
        x = referenceRect.left;
      } else if (align === "center") {
        x = referenceRect.left + (referenceRect.width - floatingRect.width) / 2;
      } else {
        x = referenceRect.right - floatingRect.width;
      }
    } else {
      if (align === "start") {
        y = referenceRect.top;
      } else if (align === "center") {
        y = referenceRect.top + (referenceRect.height - floatingRect.height) / 2;
      } else {
        y = referenceRect.bottom - floatingRect.height;
      }
    }
    return { x, y };
  }
  function getOverflow({
    x,
    y,
    floatingRect,
    padding = 0
  }) {
    const leftOverflow = x - padding;
    const topOverflow = y - padding;
    const rightOverflow = x + floatingRect.width + padding - window.innerWidth;
    const bottomOverflow = y + floatingRect.height + padding - window.innerHeight;
    return {
      left: leftOverflow < 0 ? -leftOverflow : 0,
      top: topOverflow < 0 ? -topOverflow : 0,
      right: rightOverflow > 0 ? rightOverflow : 0,
      bottom: bottomOverflow > 0 ? bottomOverflow : 0,
      any: leftOverflow < 0 || topOverflow < 0 || rightOverflow > 0 || bottomOverflow > 0
    };
  }
  function useFloating(options = {}) {
    const {
      placement = "bottom-start",
      offset = 8,
      flip = true,
      shiftPadding = 8,
      whileElementsMounted = true
    } = options;
    const referenceRef = React.useRef(null);
    const floatingRef = React.useRef(null);
    const placementRef = React.useRef(placement);
    placementRef.current = placement;
    const updateRef = React.useRef(() => {
    });
    const [floatingStyles, setFloatingStyles] = React.useState({
      position: "fixed",
      left: -9999,
      top: -9999,
      visibility: "hidden"
      // <-- importante
    });
    const compute = React.useCallback(() => {
      const refEl = referenceRef.current;
      const floatEl = floatingRef.current;
      if (!refEl || !floatEl) return;
      const referenceRect = getRect(refEl);
      const floatingRect = getRect(floatEl);
      const { base, align } = parsePlacement(placementRef.current);
      let { x, y } = computeCoords({ referenceRect, floatingRect, base, align, offset });
      let overflow = getOverflow({ x, y, floatingRect, padding: shiftPadding });
      if (flip && overflow.any) {
        const oppositeBase = opp(base);
        const { x: x2, y: y2 } = computeCoords({
          referenceRect,
          floatingRect,
          base: oppositeBase,
          align,
          offset
        });
        const overflowOpp = getOverflow({ x: x2, y: y2, floatingRect, padding: shiftPadding });
        const sumOverflow = overflow.left + overflow.top + overflow.right + overflow.bottom;
        const sumOpp = overflowOpp.left + overflowOpp.top + overflowOpp.right + overflowOpp.bottom;
        if (sumOpp < sumOverflow) {
          ({ x, y } = { x: x2, y: y2 });
          overflow = overflowOpp;
        }
      }
      const minX = shiftPadding;
      const maxX = window.innerWidth - floatingRect.width - shiftPadding;
      const minY = shiftPadding;
      const maxY = window.innerHeight - floatingRect.height - shiftPadding;
      x = clamp(x, minX, Math.max(minX, maxX));
      y = clamp(y, minY, Math.max(minY, maxY));
      setFloatingStyles({
        position: "fixed",
        left: Math.round(x),
        top: Math.round(y),
        visibility: "visible"
      });
    }, [offset, flip, shiftPadding]);
    React.useEffect(() => {
      updateRef.current = compute;
    }, [compute]);
    React.useEffect(() => {
      if (!whileElementsMounted) return;
      let roRef = null;
      const handle = () => updateRef.current();
      if (referenceRef.current && floatingRef.current) {
        roRef = new ResizeObserver(handle);
        roRef.observe(referenceRef.current);
        roRef.observe(floatingRef.current);
      }
      window.addEventListener("resize", handle);
      window.addEventListener("scroll", handle, true);
      const interval = setInterval(handle, 200);
      return () => {
        if (roRef) {
          try {
            roRef.disconnect();
          } catch {
          }
          roRef = null;
        }
        window.removeEventListener("resize", handle);
        window.removeEventListener("scroll", handle, true);
        clearInterval(interval);
      };
    }, [whileElementsMounted]);
    const setReference = React.useCallback((node) => {
      referenceRef.current = node;
      requestAnimationFrame(() => updateRef.current());
    }, []);
    const setFloating = React.useCallback((node) => {
      floatingRef.current = node;
      requestAnimationFrame(() => updateRef.current());
    }, []);
    const update = React.useCallback(() => updateRef.current(), []);
    return {
      refs: {
        setReference,
        setFloating,
        reference: referenceRef,
        floating: floatingRef
      },
      floatingStyles,
      update
    };
  }

  // virtual:/components/ui/popover.tsx
  var { useRef: useRef3, useEffect: useEffect3 } = React;
  function Popover({
    open,
    onOpenChange,
    trigger,
    children,
    placement = "bottom-start",
    offset = 8,
    flip = true,
    popoverClassName
  }) {
    const { refs, floatingStyles, update } = useFloating({
      placement,
      offset,
      flip,
      whileElementsMounted: true
    });
    React.useEffect(() => {
      if (open) update();
    }, [open, update]);
    React.useEffect(() => {
      if (!open) return;
      function handle(e) {
        const ref = refs.reference.current;
        const float = refs.floating.current;
        const target = e.target;
        if (ref && !ref.contains(target) && float && !float.contains(target)) {
          onOpenChange(false);
        }
      }
      function handleEsc(e) {
        if (e.key === "Escape") onOpenChange(false);
      }
      document.addEventListener("mousedown", handle);
      document.addEventListener("keydown", handleEsc);
      return () => {
        document.removeEventListener("mousedown", handle);
        document.removeEventListener("keydown", handleEsc);
      };
    }, [open, onOpenChange, refs]);
    return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { className: "inline-block" }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(
      "div",
      {
        ref: refs.setReference,
        onClick: () => onOpenChange(!open),
        className: "cursor-pointer"
      },
      trigger
    ), open && /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(
      "div",
      {
        ref: refs.setFloating,
        style: floatingStyles,
        className: cn(
          "z-50 rounded-md border border-border bg-background p-3 shadow-lg w-screen sm:w-auto",
          popoverClassName
        )
      },
      children
    ));
  }

  var AuthContext = React.createContext({});
  var AuthProviderClient = ({ children }) => {
    const {
      store,
      isSsr,
      user: providedUser,
      sharpifyApi
    } = React.useContext(SharpifyApi.SharpifyReact.TemplateContext);
    const [sessionId, setSessionId] = React.useState(
      () => SharpifyApi.SharpifyReact.getCookies().sessionId
    );
    const queryClient2 = ReactQuery.useQueryClient();
    if (isSsr) return children;
    const queryKey = ["current-user", providedUser?.customerId];
    const {
      data: user,
      isFetched,
      isFetching,
      refetch
    } = ReactQuery.useQuery({
      queryKey,
      queryFn: () => SharpifyApi.SharpifyReact.ReactQueryAdapter(
        sharpifyApi.api.v1.management.auth.getCurrentSession()
      ),
      initialData: providedUser,
      retry: false,
      enabled: false
    });
    React.useEffect(() => {
      (async () => {
        if (sessionId) return;
        const req = await sharpifyApi.api.v1.eCommerce.analytics.createSession({ sessionId });
        if (!req.success) return;
        setCookie({ name: "sessionId", value: req.data.id, days: 365 });
        setSessionId(req.data.id);
      })();
    }, []);
    async function logOut() {
      deleteCookie({ name: "customerAccessToken" });
      queryClient2.setQueryData(queryKey, null);
    }
    let status = "UNAUTHENTICATED";
    if (user) status = "AUTHENTICATED";
    return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(
      AuthContext.Provider,
      {
        value: {
          status,
          hasSession: !!sessionId,
          sessionId,
          user,
          refetch,
          logOut
        }
      },
      children
    );
  };
  var getAuthContext = () => {
    const { PROPERTIES_INJECT } = React.useContext(SharpifyApi.SharpifyReact.TemplateContext);

  // virtual:/components/layout/header/login/hooks/use-oauth-login.tsx
  var { useContext: useContext2, useEffect: useEffect4, useState: useState3 } = React;
  function useOauthLogin() {
    const [popupOpened, setPopupOpened] = useState3(false);
    const { store, sharpifyApi } = useContext2(SharpifyApi.SharpifyReact.TemplateContext);
    const { refetch } = useContext2(AuthContext);
    function callLogin({ platform }) {
      const width = 500;
      const height = 600;
      const left = window.screen.width / 2 - width / 2;
      const top = window.screen.height / 2 - height / 2;
      const popup = window.open(
        `${sharpifyApi.url}/api/v1/management/auth/oauth/${platform}/get-signup-url?originUrl=${window.location.origin}`,
        `${platform.toLocaleLowerCase()} Login`,
        `width=${width},height=${height},top=${top},left=${left}`
      );
      setPopupOpened(true);
      const interval = setInterval(() => {
        if (popup?.closed) {
          clearInterval(interval);
          clearInterval(intervalMessage);
          setPopupOpened(false);
          window.removeEventListener("message", receiveMessage);
        }
      }, 500);
      const intervalMessage = setInterval(() => {
        popup?.postMessage("", sharpifyApi.url);
      }, 500);
      const receiveMessage = async (event) => {
        if (event.data.code) {
          const code = event.data.code;
          const req = await sharpifyApi.api.v1.management.auth.oauthChangeCodeForToken({ code, platform });
          if (req.success) {
            setCookie({
              days: 30,
              name: "customerAccessToken",
              value: req.data.accessToken
            });
            await refetch();
          }
          popup?.close();
        }
      };
      window.addEventListener("message", receiveMessage);
    }
    return {
      callLogin,
      popupOpened
    };
  }

  // virtual:/components/ui/input-otp.tsx
  var OTPContext = React.createContext(null);
  var InputOTP = React.forwardRef(({ value = "", onChange, length = 6, containerClassName, className, disabled }, ref) => {
    const [activeIndex, setActiveIndex] = React.useState(0);
    const inputRef = React.useRef(null);
    React.useImperativeHandle(ref, () => inputRef.current);
    const slots = Array.from({ length }, (_, i) => ({
      char: value[i] || "",
      isActive: i === activeIndex,
      hasCaret: i === activeIndex
    }));
    const focusIndex = (i) => {
      if (disabled) return;
      setActiveIndex(i);
      inputRef.current?.focus();
    };
    const handleKey = (e) => {
      if (disabled) return;
      if (e.key === "Backspace") {
        e.preventDefault();
        if (value[activeIndex]) {
          onChange(value.slice(0, activeIndex) + value.slice(activeIndex + 1));
        } else if (activeIndex > 0) {
          setActiveIndex((i) => i - 1);
          onChange(value.slice(0, activeIndex - 1) + value.slice(activeIndex));
        }
      } else if (e.key === "ArrowLeft") {
        e.preventDefault();
        setActiveIndex((i) => Math.max(0, i - 1));
      } else if (e.key === "ArrowRight") {
        e.preventDefault();
        setActiveIndex((i) => Math.min(length - 1, i + 1));
      }
    };
    const handleInput = (e) => {
      if (disabled) return;
      const inputValue = e.target.value.replace(/\D/g, "");
      if (!inputValue) return;
      let chars = value.split("");
      chars[activeIndex] = inputValue[0];
      onChange(chars.join(""));
      if (activeIndex < length - 1) setActiveIndex((i) => i + 1);
      e.target.value = "";
    };
    React.useEffect(() => {
      if (!disabled) inputRef.current?.focus();
    }, [activeIndex, disabled]);
    const handlePaste = (e) => {
      if (disabled) return;
      e.preventDefault();
      const paste = e.clipboardData.getData("Text").replace(/\D/g, "");
      if (!paste) return;
      let chars = value.split("");
      for (let i = 0; i < length; i++) {
        if (paste[i]) chars[i] = paste[i];
      }
      onChange(chars.join(""));
      setActiveIndex(Math.min(length - 1, paste.length - 1));
    };
    return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(
      OTPContext.Provider,
      {
        value: {
          slots,
          activeIndex,
          focusIndex,
          handleKey,
          length,
          disabled
        }
      },
      /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { className: cn("relative flex items-center gap-2", containerClassName), onClick: () => inputRef.current?.focus() }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(
        "input",
        {
          ref: inputRef,
          type: "text",
          inputMode: "numeric",
          autoComplete: "one-time-code",
          className: "absolute opacity-0 pointer-events-none",
          onKeyDown: handleKey,
          onChange: handleInput,
          disabled,
          onPaste: handlePaste
        }
      ), slots.map((_, i) => /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(InputOTPSlot, { key: i, index: i })))
    );
  });
  InputOTP.displayName = "InputOTP";
  var InputOTPSlot = React.forwardRef(({ index, className, ...props }, ref) => {
    const ctx = React.useContext(OTPContext);
    if (!ctx) throw new Error("InputOTPSlot must be used within InputOTP");
    const { slots, focusIndex, disabled } = ctx;
    const { char, isActive, hasCaret } = slots[index];
    return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(
      "div",
      {
        ref,
        onClick: () => focusIndex(index),
        className: cn(
          "relative flex h-12 w-14 items-center justify-center border border-border rounded-md text-lg font-medium select-none transition-all",
          isActive && "ring-2 ring-primary",
          disabled && "opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed",
          className
        ),
        ...props
      },
      char,
      hasCaret && /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { className: "absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center pointer-events-none" }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { className: "h-4 w-px animate-caret-blink bg-foreground" }))
    );
  });
  InputOTPSlot.displayName = "InputOTPSlot";
  var InputOTPGroup = React.forwardRef(({ className, ...props }, ref) => /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { ref, className: cn("flex items-center gap-3", className), ...props }));
  InputOTPGroup.displayName = "InputOTPGroup";
  var InputOTPSeparator = React.forwardRef(({ className, ...props }, ref) => /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { ref, role: "separator", className: cn("mx-3 text-muted-foreground", className), ...props }, "-"));
  InputOTPSeparator.displayName = "InputOTPSeparator";

  // virtual:/lib/zod-resolver.tsx
  function toNestErrors(errors) {
    const result = {};
    const queue = [...errors];
    while (queue.length) {
      const err = queue.shift();
      const path = err.path.join(".");
      if (!result[path]) {
        if ("unionErrors" in err && err.unionErrors.length) {
          const u = err.unionErrors[0].errors[0];
          result[path] = { message: u.message, type: u.code };
        } else {
          result[path] = { message: err.message, type: err.code };
        }
      }
      if ("unionErrors" in err && err.unionErrors.length) {
        err.unionErrors.forEach((e) => e.errors.forEach((inner) => queue.push(inner)));
      }
    }
    return result;
  }
  function zodResolver(schema, context = {}, options = {}) {
    return async (data, _, formOptions) => {
      try {
        const parsed = options.mode === "sync" ? schema.parse(data) : await schema.parseAsync(data, context);
        return { values: options.raw ? data : parsed, errors: {} };
      } catch (e) {
        if (e instanceof Zod.ZodError) {
          const errors = toNestErrors([...e.errors]);
          return { values: {}, errors };
        }
        throw e;
      }
    };
  }

  // virtual:/components/layout/header/login/schemas.tsx
  var DefaultSchema = Zod.object({
    email: Zod.string().email({ message: "Email Invalido" }).max(255, { message: "Maximo de caracteres 255" }),
    code: Zod.string().min(6, { message: "C\xF2digo deve ter no minimo 6 caracteres" }).max(6)
  });

  // virtual:/lib/guest-orders.ts
  var STORAGE_KEY = "guest_orders";
  var UNSEEN_KEY = "guest_orders_unseen";
  var SEEN_IDS_KEY = "guest_orders_seen_ids";
  function getOrders() {
    try {
      const raw = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY);
      if (!raw) return [];
      const parsed = JSON.parse(raw);
      return Array.isArray(parsed) ? parsed : [];
    } catch {
      resetOrders();
      return [];
    }
  }
  function resetOrders() {
    try {
      localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, "[]");
      localStorage.setItem(UNSEEN_KEY, "0");
    } catch {
    }
  }
  function listGuestOrders() {
    return getOrders();
  }
  function getUnseenCount() {
    try {
      const raw = localStorage.getItem(UNSEEN_KEY);
      const n = parseInt(raw || "0", 10);
      return isNaN(n) ? 0 : n;
    } catch {
      return 0;
    }
  }
  function setUnseenCount(n) {
    try {
      localStorage.setItem(UNSEEN_KEY, String(Math.max(0, n)));
    } catch {
    }
  }
  function resetUnseenCount() {
    setUnseenCount(0);
  }
  function clearGuestOrders() {
    try {
      localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, "[]");
      localStorage.setItem(UNSEEN_KEY, "0");
      localStorage.removeItem(SEEN_IDS_KEY);
    } catch {
    }
  }

  // virtual:/components/layout/header/login/guest-orders-dialog.tsx
  function formatDate(dateStr) {
    try {
      const d = new Date(dateStr);
      if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return "";
      const day = String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, "0");
      const month = String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, "0");
      const year = d.getFullYear();
      const hours = String(d.getHours()).padStart(2, "0");
      const minutes = String(d.getMinutes()).padStart(2, "0");
      return `${day}/${month}/${year} \xE0s ${hours}:${minutes}`;
    } catch {
      return "";
    }
  }

  function LoginButton({
    triggerToast,
    refetch,
    sharpifyApi
  }) {
    const [loginOpen, setLoginOpen] = React.useState(false);
    const [popoverOpen, setPopoverOpen] = React.useState(false);
    const [ordersOpen, setOrdersOpen] = React.useState(false);
    const [section, setSection] = React.useState("MAIN");
    const [unseenCount, setUnseenCountState] = React.useState(0);
    React.useEffect(() => {
      try {
        setUnseenCountState(getUnseenCount());
      } catch {
      }
    }, [popoverOpen, ordersOpen]);
    React.useEffect(() => {
      const handler = () => setLoginOpen(true);
      window.addEventListener("open-login-dialog", handler);
      return () => window.removeEventListener("open-login-dialog", handler);
    }, []);
    const { callLogin, popupOpened } = useOauthLogin();
    const form = ReactHookForm.useForm({
      resolver: zodResolver(
        section === "MAIN" ? DefaultSchema.pick({ email: true }) : DefaultSchema
      ),
      mode: "onChange"
    });
    const onSubmit = form.handleSubmit(async () => {
      const data = form.watch();
      if (section === "MAIN") {
        const req2 = await sharpifyApi.api.v1.management.auth.defaultSendVerificationCodeToEmail(
          { email: data.email }
        );
        if (!req2.success)
          return triggerToast({
            message: `Ocorreu um error: ${req2.errorName}`,
            type: "error"
          });
        return setSection("VERIFY_EMAIL");
      }
      const req = await sharpifyApi.api.v1.management.auth.defaultVerifyCode({
        email: data.email,
        code: data.code
      });
      if (!req.success) {
        if (req.errorName === "InvalidCodeError")
          return triggerToast({ message: `C\xF3digo invalido!`, type: "error" });
        return triggerToast({
          message: `Ocorreu um error: ${req.errorName}`,
          type: "error"
        });
      }
      form.reset();
      setSection("MAIN");
      setLoginOpen(false);
      setCookie({
        days: 30,
        name: "customerAccessToken",
        value: req.data.accessToken
      });
      triggerToast({ message: `Usu\xE1rio logado com successo!`, type: "success" });
      await refetch();
    });
    return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(React.Fragment, null, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(Dialog, { open: loginOpen, onOpenChange: setLoginOpen }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(DialogContent, null, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { className: "space-y-4" }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(DialogHeader, null, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(DialogTitle, { className: "flex justify-center text-2xl" }, "Entre na sua conta"), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(DialogDescription, { className: "flex justify-center text-base" }, "Acesse sua conta visualizar suas compras.")), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(Form, { ...form }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("form", { onSubmit, className: "space-y-4" }, section === "MAIN" && /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(
      FormField,
      {
        name: "email",
        control: form.control,
        disabled: form.formState.isSubmitting,
        render: ({ field }) => /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(FormItem, null, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(FormLabel, null, "Email"), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(FormControl, null, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(Input, { ...field, placeholder: "exemplo@exemplo.com" })), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(FormMessage, null))
      }
    ), section === "VERIFY_EMAIL" && /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(

      {

  function Login() {

        LoginButton,
        {
          triggerToast,
          refetch,
          sharpifyApi
        }
      ),
      "user"
    ), SharpifyApi.SharpifyReact.showComponentIfTruthy(
      user,
      () => /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(
        LoggedUser,
        {
          user,
          store,
          logOut
        }
      ),
      "user"
    ));
  }

  function SocialMediaPopoverButton({
    socialMedias,
    className
  }) {
    const [open, setOpen] = React.useState(false);
    const { refs, floatingStyles } = useFloating({
      placement: "bottom-end",
      offset: 8,
      flip: true,
      shiftPadding: 8
    });
    React.useEffect(() => {
      if (!open) return;
      function handleClick(e) {
        if (refs.reference.current?.contains(e.target) || refs.floating.current?.contains(e.target))
          return;
        setOpen(false);
      }
      function handleEsc(e) {
        if (e.key === "Escape") setOpen(false);
      }
      document.addEventListener("mousedown", handleClick);
      document.addEventListener("keydown", handleEsc);
      return () => {
        document.removeEventListener("mousedown", handleClick);
        document.removeEventListener("keydown", handleEsc);
      };
    }, [open]);
    return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(React.Fragment, null, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(
      "button",
      {
        ref: refs.setReference,
        onClick: () => setOpen(!open),

  // virtual:/components/layout/plugins/top-loader.tsx
  var { useEffect: useEffect5, useRef: useRef4, useState: useState4 } = React;
  var TopLoader = () => {
    const [progress, setProgress] = useState4(0);
    const [visible, setVisible] = useState4(false);
    const intervalRef = useRef4(null);
    const start = () => {
      if (intervalRef.current) clearInterval(intervalRef.current);
      setVisible(true);
      setProgress(0);
      intervalRef.current = setInterval(() => {
        setProgress((p) => p < 90 ? p + Math.random() * 10 : p);
      }, 10);
    };
    const finish = () => {
      if (intervalRef.current) clearInterval(intervalRef.current);
      setProgress(100);
      setTimeout(() => setVisible(false), 400);
      setTimeout(() => setProgress(0), 600);
    };
    useEffect5(() => {
      window.addEventListener("load", finish);
      const handleLinkClick = (event) => {
        const target = event.target;
        if (!target) return;
        const anchor = target.closest("a");
        if (!anchor) return;
        const href = anchor.getAttribute("href");
        if (!href || href.startsWith("#")) return;
        if (href.startsWith("http")) {
          try {
            const linkUrl = new URL(href);
            if (linkUrl.host !== window.location.host) return;
          } catch {
            return;
          }
        }
        if (anchor.getAttribute("target") === "_blank") return;
        event.preventDefault();
        start();
        setTimeout(() => {
          window.location.href = href;
        }, 10);
        setTimeout(() => {
          finish();
        }, 100);
      };
      document.addEventListener("click", handleLinkClick);
      return () => {
        document.removeEventListener("click", handleLinkClick);
        window.removeEventListener("load", finish);
        if (intervalRef.current) clearInterval(intervalRef.current);
      };
    }, []);
    return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(
      "div",
      {
        className: "fixed top-0 left-0 h-[3px] w-full bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-primary/70 origin-left transition-transform duration-300 ease-out z-[9999]",
        style: {
          transform: `scaleX(${progress / 100})`,
          opacity: visible ? 1 : 0,
          transition: "transform 0.3s ease, opacity 0.3s ease"
        }
      }
    );
  };

  var FacebookPixel = () => {
    const { store, isSsr } = React.useContext(
      SharpifyApi.SharpifyReact.TemplateContext
    );
    const isEnabled = store?.pluginConfigs?.FACEBOOK_PIXEL?.isEnabled === true;
    const pixelId = String(
      store?.pluginConfigs?.FACEBOOK_PIXEL?.config?.pixelId || ""
    ).trim();
    React.useEffect(() => {
      if (!isEnabled || !pixelId) return;
      if (window.__fbPixelInitialized === pixelId) return;
      window.__fbPixelInitialized = pixelId;
      if (!window.fbq) {
        const n = function(...args) {
          n.callMethod ? n.callMethod.apply(n, args) : n.queue.push(args);
        };
        n.push = n;
        n.loaded = true;
        n.version = "2.0";
        n.queue = [];
        window.fbq = n;
        window._fbq = window._fbq || n;
      }
      const script = document.createElement("script");
      script.async = true;
      script.src = "https://connect.facebook.net/en_US/fbevents.js";
      document.head.appendChild(script);
      const fbq = window.fbq;
      fbq("init", pixelId);
      fbq("track", "PageView");
      const noscript = document.createElement("noscript");
      const img = document.createElement("img");
      img.height = 1;
      img.width = 1;
      img.style.display = "none";
      img.src = `https://www.facebook.com/tr?id=${pixelId}&ev=PageView&noscript=1`;
      noscript.appendChild(img);
      document.body.appendChild(noscript);
    }, [isEnabled, pixelId]);
    React.useEffect(() => {
      if (isSsr || !isEnabled || !pixelId) return;
      const handleAddToCart = (event) => {
        const fbq = window.fbq;
        if (!fbq) return;
        const detail = event.detail;
        fbq("track", "AddToCart", {
          content_ids: [detail.product.id],
          content_name: detail.product.name,
          content_type: "product",
          contents: [{ id: detail.product.id, quantity: 1 }],
          currency: detail.currency,
          value: detail.product.value
        });
      };
      window.addEventListener("sharpify:add-to-cart", handleAddToCart);
      return () => window.removeEventListener("sharpify:add-to-cart", handleAddToCart);
    }, [isSsr, isEnabled, pixelId]);
    React.useEffect(() => {
      if (isSsr || !isEnabled || !pixelId) return;
      const handleOrderInitialized = (event) => {
        const fbq = window.fbq;
        if (!fbq) return;
        const detail = event.detail;
        fbq(
          "track",
          "InitiateCheckout",
          {
            content_ids: detail.products.map((p) => p.id),
            content_type: "product",
            contents: detail.products.map((p) => ({ id: p.id, quantity: 1 })),
            currency: detail.currency,
            num_items: detail.products.length,
            value: detail.value
          },
          { eventID: `init_${detail.order_id}` }
        );
      };
      window.addEventListener(
        "sharpify:order-initialized",
        handleOrderInitialized
      );
      return () => window.removeEventListener(
        "sharpify:order-initialized",
        handleOrderInitialized
      );
    }, [isSsr, isEnabled, pixelId]);
    React.useEffect(() => {
      if (isSsr || !isEnabled || !pixelId) return;
      const handlePurchase = (event) => {
        const fbq = window.fbq;
        if (!fbq) return;
        const detail = event.detail;
        fbq(
          "track",
          "Purchase",
          {
            content_ids: detail.products.map((p) => p.id),
            content_type: "product",
            contents: detail.products.map((p) => ({ id: p.id, quantity: 1 })),
            currency: detail.currency,
            num_items: detail.products.length,
            value: detail.value
          },
          { eventID: `purchase_${detail.order_id}` }
        );
      };
      window.addEventListener("sharpify:purchase", handlePurchase);
      return () => window.removeEventListener("sharpify:purchase", handlePurchase);
    }, [isSsr, isEnabled, pixelId]);
    return null;
  };

  // virtual:/components/layout/plugins/tiktok-pixel.tsx
  var TIKTOK_PIXEL_SCRIPT_ID = "sharpify-tiktok-pixel-script";
  var TIKTOK_PIXEL_RUNTIME_KEY = "__sharpifyTikTokPixelInitializedId";
  function ensureTikTokPixel() {
    const runtime = window;
    runtime.TiktokAnalyticsObject = "ttq";
    let ttq = runtime.ttq;
    if (!ttq || typeof ttq.push !== "function") {
      ttq = [];
      runtime.ttq = ttq;
    }
    ttq.methods = [
      "page",
      "track",
      "identify",
      "instances",
      "debug",
      "on",
      "off",
      "once",
      "ready",
      "alias",
      "group",
      "enableCookie",
      "disableCookie",
      "holdConsent",
      "revokeConsent",
      "grantConsent"
    ];
    ttq.setAndDefer = function(target, method) {
      target[method] = function() {
        target.push([method].concat(Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments, 0)));
      };
    };
    for (let i = 0; i < ttq.methods.length; i++) {
      ttq.setAndDefer(ttq, ttq.methods[i]);
    }
    ttq.instance = function(id) {
      ttq._i = ttq._i || {};
      ttq._i[id] = ttq._i[id] || [];
      for (let i = 0; i < ttq.methods.length; i++) {
        ttq.setAndDefer(ttq._i[id], ttq.methods[i]);
      }
      return ttq._i[id];
    };
    ttq.load = function(id, options) {
      const src = "https://analytics.tiktok.com/i18n/pixel/events.js";
      const existingScript = document.getElementById(TIKTOK_PIXEL_SCRIPT_ID);
      ttq._i = ttq._i || {};
      ttq._i[id] = ttq._i[id] || [];
      ttq._i[id]._u = src;
      ttq._t = ttq._t || {};
      ttq._t[id] = +/* @__PURE__ */ new Date();
      ttq._o = ttq._o || {};
      ttq._o[id] = options || {};
      if (existingScript) return;
      const script = document.createElement("script");
      script.id = TIKTOK_PIXEL_SCRIPT_ID;
      script.async = true;
      script.src = `${src}?sdkid=${id}&lib=ttq`;
      const firstScript = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
      if (firstScript?.parentNode) {
        firstScript.parentNode.insertBefore(script, firstScript);
        return;
      }
      document.head.appendChild(script);
    };
    return ttq;
  }
  var TikTokPixel = () => {
    const { store, isSsr } = React.useContext(
      SharpifyApi.SharpifyReact.TemplateContext
    );
    const isEnabled = store?.pluginConfigs?.TIKTOK_PIXEL?.isEnabled === true;
    const pixelId = String(
      store?.pluginConfigs?.TIKTOK_PIXEL?.config?.pixelId || ""
    ).trim();
    React.useEffect(() => {
      if (isSsr) return;
      const runtime = window;
      const existingScript = document.getElementById(TIKTOK_PIXEL_SCRIPT_ID);
      if (!isEnabled || !pixelId) {
        delete runtime[TIKTOK_PIXEL_RUNTIME_KEY];
        if (existingScript?.parentNode) {
          existingScript.parentNode.removeChild(existingScript);
        }
        return;
      }
      const ttq = ensureTikTokPixel();
      if (runtime[TIKTOK_PIXEL_RUNTIME_KEY] !== pixelId) {
        if (existingScript?.parentNode) {
          existingScript.parentNode.removeChild(existingScript);
        }
        ttq.load(pixelId);
        runtime[TIKTOK_PIXEL_RUNTIME_KEY] = pixelId;
      }
      ttq.page();
    }, [isSsr, isEnabled, pixelId]);
    React.useEffect(() => {
      if (isSsr || !isEnabled || !pixelId) return;
      const handleAddToCart = (event) => {
        const runtime = window;
        const ttq = runtime.ttq;
        if (!ttq || typeof ttq.track !== "function") return;
        const detail = event.detail;
        ttq.track("AddToCart", {
          content_id: detail.product.id,
          content_name: detail.product.name,
          content_type: "product",
          value: detail.product.value,
          currency: detail.currency
        });
      };
      window.addEventListener("sharpify:add-to-cart", handleAddToCart);
      return () => {
        window.removeEventListener("sharpify:add-to-cart", handleAddToCart);
      };
    }, [isSsr, isEnabled, pixelId]);
    React.useEffect(() => {
      if (isSsr || !isEnabled || !pixelId) return;
      const handleOrderInitialized = (event) => {
        const runtime = window;
        const ttq = runtime.ttq;
        if (!ttq || typeof ttq.track !== "function") return;
        const detail = event.detail;
        ttq.track(
          "InitiateCheckout",
          {
            value: detail.value,
            currency: detail.currency,
            content_ids: detail.products.map((p) => p.id),
            content_type: "product"
          },
          { event_id: `init_${detail.order_id}` }
        );
      };
      window.addEventListener(
        "sharpify:order-initialized",
        handleOrderInitialized
      );
      return () => {
        window.removeEventListener(
          "sharpify:order-initialized",
          handleOrderInitialized
        );
      };
    }, [isSsr, isEnabled, pixelId]);
    React.useEffect(() => {
      if (isSsr || !isEnabled || !pixelId) return;
      const handlePurchase = (event) => {
        const runtime = window;
        const ttq = runtime.ttq;
        if (!ttq || typeof ttq.track !== "function") return;
        const detail = event.detail;
        ttq.track(
          "CompletePayment",
          {
            value: detail.value,
            currency: detail.currency,
            content_ids: detail.products.map((p) => p.id),
            content_type: "product"
          },
          { event_id: `purchase_${detail.order_id}` }
        );
      };
      window.addEventListener("sharpify:purchase", handlePurchase);
      return () => {
        window.removeEventListener("sharpify:purchase", handlePurchase);
      };
    }, [isSsr, isEnabled, pixelId]);
    return null;
  };

  // virtual:/components/layout/plugins/crisp.tsx
  var CrispChat = () => {
    const { store } = React.useContext(SharpifyApi.SharpifyReact.TemplateContext);
    const { user } = React.useContext(getAuthContext());
    React.useEffect(() => {
      const crispPlugin = store?.pluginConfigs?.CRISP;
      if (!crispPlugin?.isEnabled) return;
      const websiteId = crispPlugin?.config?.websiteId;
      if (!websiteId) return;
      window.$crisp = window.$crisp || [];
      window.CRISP_WEBSITE_ID = websiteId;
      const script = document.createElement("script");
      script.src = "https://client.crisp.chat/l.js";
      script.async = true;
      document.head.appendChild(script);
      if (user) {
        if (user.customerId)
          window.$crisp.push(["set", "user:id", [String(user.customerId)]]);
        if (user.email) window.$crisp.push(["set", "user:email", [user.email]]);
        if (user.username)
          window.$crisp.push(["set", "user:nickname", [user.username]]);
        if (user.avatar) window.$crisp.push(["set", "user:avatar", [user.avatar]]);
      }
      return () => {
        document.head.removeChild(script);
      };
    }, [user]);
    return null;
  };

  // virtual:/components/layout/plugins/affiliate.tsx
  var SetAffiliate = () => {
    const { sharpifyApi, isSsr } = React.useContext(SharpifyApi.SharpifyReact.TemplateContext);
    const { sessionId } = React.useContext(getAuthContext());
    React.useEffect(() => {
      if (isSsr) return;
      if (!sessionId) return;
      const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
      const affiliateCodeFromParam = params.get("ref");
      const currentAffiliateCode = SharpifyApi.SharpifyReact.getCookies()?.affiliateCode;
      const affiliateCodeToUse = affiliateCodeFromParam || currentAffiliateCode;
      if (!affiliateCodeToUse) return;
      (async () => {
        if (affiliateCodeFromParam && currentAffiliateCode !== affiliateCodeFromParam) {
          const req = await sharpifyApi.api.v1.pricing.affiliate.validateAffiliateCode({
            code: affiliateCodeFromParam
          });
          if (!req.success) return;
          setCookie({
            name: "affiliateCode",
            value: affiliateCodeFromParam,
            days: req.data.cookieExpirationInDays
          });
        }
        await sharpifyApi.api.v1.eCommerce.analytics.linkAffiliateToSession({
          sessionId,
          code: affiliateCodeToUse
        });
      })();
    }, [sharpifyApi, isSsr, sessionId]);
    return null;
  };

  // virtual:/components/layout/plugins/tawk-to.tsx
  var TawkChat = () => {
    const { store } = React.useContext(SharpifyApi.SharpifyReact.TemplateContext);
    const { user } = React.useContext(getAuthContext());
    React.useEffect(() => {
      const tawkPlugin = store?.pluginConfigs.TAWK_TO;
      if (!tawkPlugin?.isEnabled) return;
      const propertyId = tawkPlugin?.config?.propertyId;
      const widgetId = tawkPlugin?.config?.widgetId;
      if (!propertyId || !widgetId) return;
      window.Tawk_API = window.Tawk_API || {};
      window.Tawk_LoadStart = /* @__PURE__ */ new Date();
      const script = document.createElement("script");
      script.src = `https://embed.tawk.to/${propertyId}/${widgetId}`;
      script.async = true;
      document.head.appendChild(script);
      script.onload = () => {
        const Tawk_API = window?.Tawk_API;
        if (user && Tawk_API && Tawk_API?.setAttributes) {
          Tawk_API.setAttributes(
            {
              id: user.customerId ? String(user.customerId) : void 0,
              name: user.username || void 0,
              email: user.email || void 0
            },
            function(error) {
              console.error("Erro ao setar atributos no Tawk:", error);
            }
          );
        }
      };
      return () => {
        document.head.removeChild(script);
      };
    }, [user]);
    return null;
  };

      return () => {

      };
    }, [store?.pluginConfigs?.MICROSOFT_CLARITY]);
    return null;
  };

      };

  };

  function StoreStructuredData({ store }) {
    const siteUrl = String(store.url || "").replace(/\/+$/, "");
    if (!siteUrl) return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(React.Fragment, null);
    const organization = {
      "@context": "https://schema.org",

      name: String(store.info.name),

        "query-input": "required name=search_term_string"

  }
  function Layout({
    children,
    store,
    user,
    PROPERTIES_INJECT,
    isSsr = false
  }) {
    const sharpifyApi = new SharpifyApi.default({
      apiKey: "",

      // baseWebsocketUrl: "http://localhost:1000"
    });
    if (!isSsr) {
      PROPERTIES_INJECT.context_cartContext = CartContext;
      PROPERTIES_INJECT.context_toastContext = ToastContext;
      PROPERTIES_INJECT.context_authContext = AuthContext;
    }
    React.useEffect(() => {
      if (isSsr) return;
      if (PROPERTIES_INJECT.variables?.appConfig?.blockf12 !== "YES") return;
      const handleKeyDown = (e) => {
        if (e.key === "F12" || e.ctrlKey && e.shiftKey && ["I", "i", "J", "j", "C", "c"].includes(e.key) || e.ctrlKey && ["U", "u"].includes(e.key)) {
          e.preventDefault();
          e.stopPropagation();
        }
      };
      const handleContextMenu = (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
      };
      let devtoolsOpen = false;
      const threshold = 160;
      const checkDevTools = () => {
        const widthDiff = window.outerWidth - window.innerWidth > threshold;
        const heightDiff = window.outerHeight - window.innerHeight > threshold;
        if (widthDiff || heightDiff) {
          if (!devtoolsOpen) {
          }
        } else {
          devtoolsOpen = false;
        }
      };
      const interval = setInterval(checkDevTools, 1e3);
      document.addEventListener("keydown", handleKeyDown);
      document.addEventListener("contextmenu", handleContextMenu);
      return () => {
        clearInterval(interval);
        document.removeEventListener("keydown", handleKeyDown);
        document.removeEventListener("contextmenu", handleContextMenu);
      };
    }, [isSsr]);
    return /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(QueryClientProvider, { client: queryClient }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(
      SharpifyApi.SharpifyReact.TemplateContext.Provider,
      {
        value: { store, sharpifyApi, PROPERTIES_INJECT, user, isSsr }
      },
      /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(ToastProvider, { isSsr }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(CartProviders, null, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(AuthProviderClient, null, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(PluginsProvider, null, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(StoreStructuredData, { store }), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(Clip, null), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("div", { className: "overflow-x-clip " }, /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(Header, null), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement("main", { id: "main-content", className: "md:container p-3" }, children), /* @__PURE__ */ React.createElement(Footer, null))))))
    ));
